country_event = { # Laguna del Desierto
	id = LATAM.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event LATAM.1" }
	title = LATAM.1.t
	desc = LATAM.1.desc
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Christmas War happens
		name = LATAM.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 3
			modifier = {
				NOT = { CHL_argentina_friendly_government_temp = yes }
				factor = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = CHL_SKELETON_CHRISTMAS_WAR
					option = CHL_SKELETON_CHRISTMAS_WAR_NO
				}
			}
		}

		ARG = { transfer_state = 1585 set_country_flag = christmas_war_preparation }
		CHL = {
			set_country_flag = christmas_war_preparation
			set_cosmetic_tag = CHL_1965
			country_event = { # Christmas War
				id = LATAM.20
				days = 47
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				army_funding_maximal_increase_high = yes
				army_funding_maximal_increase_med = yes
				army_funding_minimal_increase_high = yes
				army_funding_minimal_increase_med = yes
			}
		}

		every_country = {
			limit = { is_ai = no }
			news_event = {
				id = LATAM_news.2
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Christmas War averted
		name = LATAM.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				CHL_argentina_friendly_government_temp = yes
				factor = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CHL_SKELETON_CHRISTMAS_WAR
						option = CHL_SKELETON_CHRISTMAS_WAR_ARG
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CHL_SKELETON_CHRISTMAS_WAR
						option = CHL_SKELETON_CHRISTMAS_WAR_HOLD
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CHL_SKELETON_CHRISTMAS_WAR
						option = CHL_SKELETON_CHRISTMAS_WAR_RETAKE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CHL_SKELETON_CHRISTMAS_WAR
						option = CHL_SKELETON_CHRISTMAS_WAR_CHL
					}
				}
			}
		}

		ARG = { transfer_state = 1585 }
		CHL = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = CHL_1965
			hidden_effect = {
				army_funding_maximal_increase_med = yes
				army_funding_minimal_increase_med = yes
			}
		}

		every_country = {
			limit = { is_ai = no }
			news_event = {
				id = LATAM_news.1
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Rettig Inauguration
	id = LATAM.2
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event LATAM.2" }
	title = LATAM.2.t
	desc = LATAM.2.desc
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		every_country = {
			limit = { is_ai = no }
			news_event = { # Chile Rettig Elected
				id = LATAM_news.20
			}
		}
		BRA = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader = { character = BRA_Carlos_Lacerda ruling_only = yes } }
				country_event = {
					id = BRA_latam_reactions.1
					days = 3
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader = { character = BRA_Adhemar_de_Barros ruling_only = yes } }
				country_event = {
					id = BRA_latam_reactions.15
					days = 3
				}
			}
		}
		CHL = {
			CHL_Eduardo_Frei = { remove_country_leader_role = { ideology = liberalism_christian_liberalism_subtype } }
			retire_ideology_leader = progressivism
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = CHL_Eduardo_Frei
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					ideology = progressivism_christian_progressivism_subtype
					expire = "1980.1.1.1"
					traits = {}
				}
			}
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			fill_empty_minister = yes
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = progressivism
				long_name = CHL_PDC_party_long
				name = CHL_PDC_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = liberalism
				long_name = CHL_FDC_radicales_party_long
				name = CHL_FDC_radicales_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = liberal_conservatism
				long_name = CHL_FDC_party_long
				name = CHL_FDC_party
			}
			retire_country_leader = yes
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = liberalism
				popularity = 0.11
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = progressivism
				popularity = 0.06
			}
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = CHL_Raul_Rettig
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					ideology = liberalism_liberal_radicalism_subtype
					expire = "1980.1.1.1"
					traits = {}
				}
			}
			meta_effect = { #sets up next election date in country ui
				text = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = liberalism
						last_election = "[current_election_date]"
						elections_allowed = yes
						election_frequency = 48
					}
				}
				current_election_date = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
			}
			remove_ideas = CHL_idea_political_fragmentation_alessandri_1
			country_event = {
				id = LATAM.27
				days = 1024
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Cautinazo
	id = LATAM.7
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event LATAM.7" }
	title = LATAM.7.t
	desc = LATAM.7.desc
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		CHL = {
			remove_ideas = CHL_idea_agrarian_timebomb
			add_ideas = CHL_idea_rural_collapse_dummy
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = CHL_rural_collapse }
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = { is_ai = no }
			news_event = {
				id = LATAM_news.19
				days = 1
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			66 = { # Alessandri resigns
				country_event = { id = LATAM.32 days = 15 }
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CHL_SKELETON_ALESSANDRI_TERM
						option = CHL_SKELETON_ALESSANDRI_TERM_STAYS
					}
				}
			}
			34 = { # Alessandri stays
				country_event = { id = LATAM.31 days = 478 }
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CHL_SKELETON_ALESSANDRI_TERM
						option = CHL_SKELETON_ALESSANDRI_TERM_RESIGNS
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Andean Pact
	id = LATAM.8
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event LATAM.8" }
	title = LATAM.8.t
	desc = LATAM.8.desc
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = { PRU = { has_country_leader = { character = PRU_Fernando_Belaunde_Terry ruling_only = yes } } }

	option = {
		name = LATAM.8.a
		# Philippi President
		if = {
			limit = { CHL = { has_country_leader = { character = CHL_Julio_Philippi ruling_only = yes } } }
			# Very cool, good friends
			ADN = { set_country_flag = HAS_ECON_SPHERE }
			PRU = { econ_join_sphere_ADN = yes set_country_flag = joined_andean_pact }
			CHL = { econ_join_sphere_ADN = yes set_country_flag = joined_andean_pact }
			if = {
				limit = {
					BOL = {
						has_idea = BOL_Chilean_Contracts
					}
				}
				BOL = { remove_ideas = BOL_Chilean_Contracts }
				BOL = { econ_join_sphere_ADN = yes set_country_flag = joined_andean_pact }
			}
			AAC = { econ_join_sphere_ADN = yes set_country_flag = joined_andean_pact }
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				news_event = { # Andean Pact
					id = LATAM_news.72
				}
			}
			#BRA = {
			#	country_event = {
			#		id = LATAM.10
			#		days = 14
			#	}
			#}
		}
		# Prat President
		else_if = {
			limit = { CHL = { has_country_leader = { character = CHL_Jorge_Prat ruling_only = yes } } }
			# It's going to be difficult
			random_list = {
				30 = {
					#modifier = {
					#	factor = 0
					#	has_game_rule = { rule = ANDEAN_PACT_CREATION option = ANDEAN_PACT_CREATION_NO }
					#}
					ADN = { set_country_flag = HAS_ECON_SPHERE }
					CHL = { set_country_flag = HAS_ECON_SPHERE } #Faux
					PRU = { econ_join_sphere_ADN = yes set_country_flag = joined_andean_pact }
					CHL = { econ_join_sphere_ADN = yes set_country_flag = joined_andean_pact }
					if = {
						limit = {
							BOL = {
								has_idea = BOL_Chilean_Contracts
							}
						}
						BOL = { remove_ideas = BOL_Chilean_Contracts }
						BOL = { econ_join_sphere_ADN = yes set_country_flag = joined_andean_pact }
					}
					AAC = { econ_join_sphere_ADN = yes set_country_flag = joined_andean_pact }
					every_country = {
						limit = { is_ai = no }
						news_event = { # Andean Pact
							id = LATAM_news.72
						}
					}
					#BRA = {
					#	country_event = {
					#		id = LATAM.10
					#		days = 14
					#	}
					#}
				}
				70 = {
					#modifier = {
					#	factor = 0
					#	has_game_rule = { rule = ANDEAN_PACT_CREATION option = ANDEAN_PACT_CREATION_YES }
					#}
				}
			}
		}
		# Frei President
		else_if = {
			limit = { CHL = { has_country_leader = { character = CHL_Eduardo_Frei ruling_only = yes } } }
			# This presents some problems, but they'll get along well
			ADN = { set_country_flag = HAS_ECON_SPHERE }
			CHL = { set_country_flag = HAS_ECON_SPHERE } #Faux
			PRU = { econ_join_sphere_ADN = yes set_country_flag = joined_andean_pact }
			CHL = { econ_join_sphere_ADN = yes set_country_flag = joined_andean_pact }
			if = {
				limit = {
					BOL = {
						has_idea = BOL_Chilean_Contracts
					}
				}
				BOL = { remove_ideas = BOL_Chilean_Contracts }
				BOL = { econ_join_sphere_ADN = yes set_country_flag = joined_andean_pact }
			}
			AAC = { econ_join_sphere_ADN = yes set_country_flag = joined_andean_pact }
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				news_event = { # Andean Pact
					id = LATAM_news.72
				}
			}
			#BRA = {
			#	country_event = {
			#		id = LATAM.10
			#		days = 14
			#	}
			#}
		}

		every_country = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = joined_andean_pact }

			set_temp_variable = { gdp_growth_temp = 0.3 }
			econ_gdp_growth_change = yes

			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				add_resource = {
					type = power
					amount = 3
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { pus_temp = 2 }
			econ_pus_change = yes
		}
	}
}

		custom_effect_tooltip = LATAM.10_tt_a

country_event = { # Joining Andean Pact
	id = LATAM.16
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event LATAM.16" }
	title = LATAM.16.t
	desc = LATAM.16.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_handshake

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = LATAM.16.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = LATAM.16_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { temp_bill = token:BRA_ENTRY_INTO_THE_ANDEAN_PACT }
			if = { # Lott
				limit = { has_country_leader = { character = BRA_Henrique_Teixeira_Lott ruling_only = yes } }
				set_variable = { BRA_pl_ptb_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.5 }
				set_variable = { BRA_pl_psd_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.7 }
				set_variable = { BRA_pl_udn_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.0 }
				set_variable = { BRA_pl_psp_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.2 }
				set_variable = { BRA_pl_prp_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.0 }
			}
			else_if = { # Quadros
				limit = { has_country_leader = { character = BRA_Janio_Quadros ruling_only = yes } }
				set_variable = { BRA_pl_ptb_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.1 }
				set_variable = { BRA_pl_psd_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.15 }
				set_variable = { BRA_pl_udn_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.5 }
				set_variable = { BRA_pl_psp_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.1 }
				set_variable = { BRA_pl_prp_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.0 }
			}
			else_if = { # Kubitschek
				limit = { has_country_leader = { character = BRA_Juscelino_Kubitschek ruling_only = yes } }
				set_variable = { BRA_pl_ptb_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.5 }
				set_variable = { BRA_pl_psd_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.7 }
				set_variable = { BRA_pl_udn_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.0 }
				set_variable = { BRA_pl_psp_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.2 }
				set_variable = { BRA_pl_prp_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.0 }
			}
			else_if = { # Lacerda
				limit = { has_country_leader = { character = BRA_Carlos_Lacerda ruling_only = yes } }
				set_variable = { BRA_pl_ptb_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.1 }
				set_variable = { BRA_pl_psd_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.1 }
				set_variable = { BRA_pl_udn_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.5 }
				set_variable = { BRA_pl_psp_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.3 }
				set_variable = { BRA_pl_prp_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.0 }
			}
			else_if = { # Adhemar
				limit = { has_country_leader = { character = BRA_Adhemar_de_Barros ruling_only = yes } }
				set_variable = { BRA_pl_ptb_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.2 }
				set_variable = { BRA_pl_psd_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.2 }
				set_variable = { BRA_pl_udn_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.3 }
				set_variable = { BRA_pl_psp_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.8 }
				set_variable = { BRA_pl_prp_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.0 }
			}
			else_if = { # Goulart
				limit = { has_country_leader = { character = BRA_Joao_Goulart ruling_only = yes } }
				set_variable = { BRA_pl_ptb_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.75 }
				set_variable = { BRA_pl_psd_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.5 }
				set_variable = { BRA_pl_udn_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.0 }
				set_variable = { BRA_pl_psp_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.2 }
				set_variable = { BRA_pl_prp_support_bill@var:temp_bill = 0.0 }
			}
			BRA_initialize_bill = yes
			set_variable = { BRA_pl_vote_days@var:temp_bill = 28 }
			BRA_call_bill_vote = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Christmas War begins
	id = LATAM.20
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event LATAM.20" }
	title = LATAM.20.t
	desc = LATAM.20.desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = LATAM.20.a

		set_global_flag = christmas_war_ocurred
		set_global_flag = christmas_war_happening
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_game_rule = {
					rule = CHL_SKELETON_CHRISTMAS_WAR
					option = CHL_SKELETON_CHRISTMAS_WAR_HOLD
				}
			}
			start_border_war = {
				change_state_after_war = no
				attacker = {
					state = 1593
					num_provinces = 1
					on_win = LATAM.22
					on_lose = LATAM.22
					on_cancel = LATAM.22
				}

				defender = {
					state = 1585
					num_provinces = 1
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CHL_SKELETON_CHRISTMAS_WAR
						option = CHL_SKELETON_CHRISTMAS_WAR_RETAKE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CHL_SKELETON_CHRISTMAS_WAR
						option = CHL_SKELETON_CHRISTMAS_WAR_CHL
					}
				}
			}
			start_border_war = {
				change_state_after_war = no
				attacker = {
					state = 1593
					num_provinces = 1
					on_win = LATAM.21
					on_lose = LATAM.21
					on_cancel = LATAM.21
				}

				defender = {
					state = 1585
					num_provinces = 1
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			start_border_war = {
				change_state_after_war = no
				attacker = {
					state = 1593
					num_provinces = 1
					on_win = LATAM.21
					on_lose = LATAM.22
					on_cancel = LATAM.22
				}

				defender = {
					state = 1585
					num_provinces = 1
				}
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = { is_ai = no }
			news_event = {
				id = LATAM_news.59
			}
		}
	}
}

						option = CHL_SKELETON_CHRISTMAS_WAR_ARG

				start_border_war = {

					attacker = {

						num_provinces = 1
						on_win = LATAM.23
						on_lose = LATAM.23
						on_cancel = LATAM.23
					}

						num_provinces = 1
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CHL_SKELETON_CHRISTMAS_WAR
						option = CHL_SKELETON_CHRISTMAS_WAR_HOLD
					}
				}
				start_border_war = {

country_event = { # Viaux Coup check
	id = LATAM.27
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event LATAM.27" }
	title = LATAM.27.t
	desc = LATAM.27.desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = LATAM.27.a
		random_list = {
			50 = { # Coup Successful
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CHL_SKELETON_VIAUX_COUP
						option = CHL_SKELETON_VIAUX_COUP_FAILS
					}
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = CHL_fascist
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = CHL_Roberto_Viaux
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						desc = "POLITICS_ROBERTO_VIAUX_DESC"
						ideology = fascism_revolutionary_nationalism_subtype
						expire = "1990.1.1.1"
						traits = {
						}
					}
				}
				set_politics = { ruling_party = fascism elections_allowed = no }
				econ_leave_sphere = yes
				remove_ideas = CHL_idea_economic_subservience
				AAC = { econ_leave_sphere = yes }
				clr_country_flag = HAS_ECON_SPHERE
				if = {
					limit = { PRU = { check_variable = { ECON_SPHERE_LEADER = ADN } } }
					econ_leave_sphere = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = KOM_socintern_associate }
					remove_ideas = KOM_socintern_associate
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = KOM_socintern_member }
					remove_ideas = KOM_socintern_member
				}
				clr_country_flag = SOCINTERN_MEMBER

				add_popularity = {
					ideology = fascism
					popularity = 0.21
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = despotism
					popularity = 0.05
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = paternalism
					popularity = 0.05
				}

				set_party_name = {
					ideology = fascism
					long_name = CHL_fascism_party_viaux_long
					name = CHL_fascism_party_viaux
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = despotism
					long_name = CHL_despotism_party_viaux_long
					name = CHL_despotism_party_viaux
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = paternalism
					long_name = CHL_paternalism_party_viaux_long
					name = CHL_paternalism_party_viaux
				}
				if = {
					limit = { ARG = { has_country_leader = { character = ARG_Juan_Domingo_Peron ruling_only = yes } } }
					set_variable = { TNO_SA_influence^global.UNALIGNED = 25 }
					set_variable = { TNO_SA_influence^global.BRAZIL = 20 }
					set_variable = { TNO_SA_influence^global.ARGENTINA = 55 }
				}
				else = {
					set_variable = { TNO_SA_influence^global.UNALIGNED = 65 }
					set_variable = { TNO_SA_influence^global.BRAZIL = 0 }
					set_variable = { TNO_SA_influence^global.ARGENTINA = 35 }
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = { is_ai = no }
					news_event = {
						id = LATAM_news.114
					}
				}
			}
			50 = { # Countercoup
				modifier = {
					factor = 0
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = CHL_SKELETON_VIAUX_COUP
						option = CHL_SKELETON_VIAUX_COUP_SUCCESS
					}
				}
				add_stability = 0.1
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = fascism
					popularity = -0.1
				}
				set_variable = { TNO_SA_influence^global.UNALIGNED = 35 }
				set_variable = { TNO_SA_influence^global.BRAZIL = 60 }
				set_variable = { TNO_SA_influence^global.ARGENTINA = 5 }
				every_country = {
					limit = { is_ai = no }
					news_event = {
						id = LATAM_news.116
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

					}
				}
				country_event = { id = LATAM_bolivia_mining_wars_epilogue.26 days = 14 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					has_country_leader = { 
						character = BRA_Adhemar_de_Barros
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = LATAM_bolivia_mining_wars_epilogue.27 days = 14 }
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = { is_ai = no }
			news_event = { id = LATAM_news.274 hours = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = { # Torres wins
		name = LATAM_bolivia_crisis.111.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = BOL_POLITICS_1967
						option = BOL_POLITICS_1967_GUEVARA
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = BOL_POLITICS_1967
						option = BOL_POLITICS_1967_LECHIN
					}
				}
			}
		}
		BOL_Juan_Jose_Torres = {
			promote_character = despotism_military_socialism_subtype
		}
		set_politics = { ruling_party = despotism }
		set_popularities = {
			communist = 18
			liberalism = 4
			liberal_conservatism = 3
			paternalism = 3
			paternalism_1 = 8
			despotism = 47
			despotism_2 = 7
			fascism = 8
			fascism_1 = 2
		}
		BRA = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					has_country_leader = { 
						character = BRA_Carlos_Lacerda
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = LATAM_bolivia_mining_wars_epilogue.28 days = 14 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 
					has_country_leader = { 
						character = BRA_Adhemar_de_Barros
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = LATAM_bolivia_mining_wars_epilogue.29 days = 14 }
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = { is_ai = no }
			news_event = { id = LATAM_news.275 hours = 1 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { TNO_economy_subtype_temp = token:Econ_Subtype_Socialized_Economy }
		econ_subtype_change = yes
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = BOL_The_Popular_Assembly
			add_idea = BOL_A_Revolutionary_Dictatorship
		}
	}

country_event = { #
	id = LATAM_cayenne.6
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event LATAM_cayenne.6" }
	title = LATAM_cayenne.6.t
	desc = LATAM_cayenne.6.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_BRA_letter

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = LATAM_cayenne.6.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_cayenne_proxy_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = LATAM_cayenne.9
				days = 110
			}
			TNO_fopo_add_cayenne_referendum_tab = yes
			TNO_fopo_setup_cayenne_referendum = yes
			set_temp_variable = { alert_id = token:Alert_LATAM_Cayenne_Referendum }
			add_TNO_alert_unless_exists = yes

			if = {
				limit = {
					BRA = {
						has_country_leader = {
							character = BRA_Adhemar_de_Barros
							ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
				}
				USA = {
					country_event = USA_FBI_LATAM.14
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #
	id = LATAM_cayenne.8
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event LATAM_cayenne.8" }
	title = LATAM_cayenne.8.t
	desc = LATAM_cayenne.8.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_BRA_lobster_dinner

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = LATAM_cayenne.8.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = BRA_adhemar_moneybags_category_allowed }
			set_temp_variable = { slush_amount = 2 }
			BRA_adhemar_spend_slush_fund = yes
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { temp_econ_spending_amount = 0.04 }
			econ_spend_money_once_effect_raw_money = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = { GUC.referendum_legitimacy_temp = 5 }
		BRA_Cayenne_Legitimacy_Change = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = LATAM_cayenne.8.b
	}
}

#Cayenne referendum results
country_event = { # Golden Victory Scenario
	id = LATAM_cayenne_endings.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event LATAM_cayenne_endings.1" }
	title = LATAM_cayenne_endings.1.t
	desc = LATAM_cayenne_endings.1.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_election

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = LATAM_cayenne_endings.1.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = BRA_cayenne_golden_ending_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = LATAM_cayenne_endings.2
				days = 90
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				news_event = {
					id = LATAM_news.223
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				BRA_Carlos_Lacerda = {
					is_country_leader = yes
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { Lacerda_Success_Meter = 1 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Golden Victory Scenario
	id = LATAM_cayenne_endings.2
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event LATAM_cayenne_endings.2" }
	title = LATAM_cayenne_endings.2.t
	desc = LATAM_cayenne_endings.2.desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = LATAM_cayenne_endings.2.a
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = LATAM_cayenne_endings.3
				days = 270
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Golden Victory Scenario
	id = LATAM_cayenne_endings.3
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event LATAM_cayenne_endings.3" }
	title = LATAM_cayenne_endings.3.t
	desc = LATAM_cayenne_endings.3.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_BRA_justin_catayee

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = LATAM_cayenne_endings.3.a
		hidden_effect = {
			BRA = {
				annex_country = {
					target = GUC
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = { is_core_of = GUC }
					add_core_of = BRA
					remove_core_of = GUC
				}
			}
			remove_from_array = {
				array = global.TNO_SA_cold_war_nations
				value = GUC
			}
			310 = {
				set_compliance = 60
				set_variable = { TNO_admin_title = 16 }
			}
			2443 = {
				set_compliance = 60
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				news_event = {
					id = LATAM_news.224
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Legitimacy Fail Scenario
	id = LATAM_cayenne_endings.15
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event LATAM_cayenne_endings.15" }
	title = LATAM_cayenne_endings.15.t
	desc = LATAM_cayenne_endings.15.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_BRA_celebration

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = LATAM_cayenne_endings.15.a
		hidden_effect = {
			BRA = {
				end_puppet = GUC
				set_autonomy = {
					target = GUC
					autonomy_state = autonomy_free
				}
			}
			GUC = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = GUC_OAS
				meta_effect = { #sets up next election date in country ui
					text = {
						set_politics = {
							ruling_party = despotism
							last_election = "[current_election_date]"
							elections_allowed = yes
							election_frequency = 48
						}
					}
					current_election_date = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
				}
				econ_leave_sphere = yes
				set_popularities = {
					despotism = 100
				}
				remove_ideas = GUC_Brazilian_Immigration
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = despotism
					long_name = GUC_OAS_Mandate_party_long
					name = GUC_OAS_Mandate_party
				}
				promote_character = {
					character = GUC_OAS_Mandate
					ideology = despotism_interim_government_subtype
				}
				set_variable = { TNO_SA_influence^global.BRAZIL = 0 }
				set_variable = { TNO_SA_influence^global.USA = 100 }
				SA_set_alignment = yes
				if = {
					limit = { has_war_with = ARG }
					white_peace = ARG
				}
				leave_faction = yes
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = LATAM_cayenne_endings.16
				days = 365
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Legitimacy Fail Scenario
	id = LATAM_cayenne_endings.16
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event LATAM_cayenne_endings.16" }
	title = LATAM_cayenne_endings.16.t
	desc = LATAM_cayenne_endings.16.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_BRA_justin_catayee

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = LATAM_cayenne_endings.16.a
		hidden_effect = {
			GUC = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = GUC_INDP
				meta_effect = { #sets up next election date in country ui
					text = {
						set_politics = {
							ruling_party = progressivism
							last_election = "[current_election_date]"
							elections_allowed = yes
							election_frequency = 48
						}
					}
					current_election_date = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
				}
				remove_ideas = OFN_Observer
				add_ideas = OFN_Dependent_Member
				econ_join_sphere_USA = yes
				set_popularities = {
					socialist = 4
					progressivism = 70
					liberal_conservatism = 26
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = progressivism
					long_name = GUC_socialist_party_long
					name = GUC_socialist_party
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = socialist
					long_name = GUC_socialist_fnlg_party_long
					name = GUC_socialist_fnlg_party
				}
				retire_ideology_leader = socialist
				promote_character = {
					character = GUC_Leon_Gontran_Damas
					ideology = socialist_subtype
				}
				promote_character = {
					character = GUC_Justin_Catayee
					ideology = progressivism_reformist_socialism_subtype
				}
			}
			USA = { add_to_faction = GUC }
			add_to_array = { global.OFN_members = GUC }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				news_event = {
					id = LATAM_news.227
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

					text = {
						set_politics = {
							ruling_party = progressivism
							last_election = "[current_election_date]"
							elections_allowed = yes
							election_frequency = 48
						}
					}
					current_election_date = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
				}
				remove_ideas = OFN_Observer
				add_ideas = OFN_Dependent_Member
				econ_join_sphere_USA = yes
				set_popularities = {
					socialist = 4
					progressivism = 70
					liberal_conservatism = 26
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = progressivism
					long_name = GUC_socialist_party_long
					name = GUC_socialist_party
				}
				set_party_name = {
					ideology = socialist
					long_name = GUC_socialist_fnlg_party_long
					name = GUC_socialist_fnlg_party
				}
				retire_ideology_leader = socialist
				promote_character = {
					character = GUC_Leon_Gontran_Damas
					ideology = socialist_subtype
				}
				promote_character = {
					character = GUC_Justin_Catayee
					ideology = progressivism_reformist_socialism_subtype
				}
			}
			USA = { add_to_faction = GUC }
			add_to_array = { global.OFN_members = GUC }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				news_event = {
					id = LATAM_news.227
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#South Atlantic War events

country_event = { # Debug scenario setter
	id = LATAM_south_atlantic_war.0
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event LATAM_south_atlantic_war.0" }
	title = LATAM_south_atlantic_war.0.t
	desc = LATAM_south_atlantic_war.0.desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # brazil vs argentina only
		name = LATAM_south_atlantic_war.0.a
		hidden_effect = {
			ARG = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = BRA
					type = annex_everything
				}
				create_faction	= Argentina_Military_Alliance
				TNO_fopo_add_south_american_war_tab = yes
			}
			BRA = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = ARG
					type = annex_everything
				}
				leave_faction = yes
				create_faction_from_template = { name = Brazil_Military_Alliance icon = GFX_BRA_faction_member template = faction_template_generic }
				add_faction_goal_slot = { category = short_term  value = -10 }
				add_faction_goal_slot = { category = medium_term value = -10 }
				add_faction_goal_slot = { category = long_term   value = -10 }
				TNO_fopo_add_south_american_war_tab = yes
			}
			set_temp_variable = { TNO_temp_super_event = token:SE_SOUTH_ATLANTIC_WAR }
			TNO_fire_super_event = yes
			set_global_flag = TNO_south_american_war_ongoing

			set_variable = { global.SATW_Escalation = 25 }
			set_variable = { global.SATW_BRA_Exhaustion = 0 }
			set_variable = { global.SATW_ARG_Exhaustion = 0 }

			if = {
				limit = {
					BRA = {
						has_country_leader = {
							character = BRA_Janio_Quadros
							ruling_only = yes
						}
					}
				}
				set_variable = { USA.SATW_Alignment = 25 }
				set_variable = { JAP.SATW_Alignment = 25 }
				set_variable = { GER.SATW_Alignment = 25 }
			}
			else = {
				set_variable = { USA.SATW_Alignment = 35 }
				set_variable = { JAP.SATW_Alignment = 20 }
				set_variable = { GER.SATW_Alignment = 15 }
			}
			set_variable = { global.SATW_skull_frame = 2 }
			set_variable = { global.SATW_flag_frame_ARG = 1 }
			set_variable = { global.SATW_flag_frame_BRA = 1 }

			ARG = { set_political_power = BRA.political_power }
			BRA = { activate_mission = SATW_ticker_mission }
			280 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = SATW_amazon_hinderances_better } }
			495 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = SATW_amazon_hinderances } }
			1479 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = SATW_amazon_hinderances } }
			1480 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = SATW_amazon_hinderances } }
			1481 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = SATW_amazon_hinderances } }
			1531 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = SATW_amazon_hinderances_better } }
			2514 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = SATW_amazon_hinderances } }
			ARG = { hidden_effect = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = ARG_SATW_foreign_support_dynmod } } }
			BRA = { hidden_effect = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = BRA_SATW_foreign_support_dynmod } } }
			force_update_dynamic_modifier = yes
			set_variable = { BRA.SATW_foreign_pu = 5 }
			set_variable = { ARG.SATW_foreign_pu = 5 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_global_flag = COL_conservatives_won }
				BRA = { country_event = { id = LATAM_south_atlantic_war.8 days = 14 } }
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { is_ai = no }
				news_event = { id = LATAM_news.230 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # brazil vs argentina + paraguay + santa cruz
		name = LATAM_south_atlantic_war.0.b
		hidden_effect = {
			ARG = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = BRA
					type = annex_everything
				}
				create_faction	= Argentina_Military_Alliance
				TNO_fopo_add_south_american_war_tab = yes
				add_to_faction = PAR
				add_to_faction = STC
			}
			BRA = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = ARG
					type = annex_everything
				}
				leave_faction = yes
				create_faction_from_template = { name = Brazil_Military_Alliance icon = GFX_BRA_faction_member template = faction_template_generic }
				add_faction_goal_slot = { category = short_term  value = -10 }
				add_faction_goal_slot = { category = medium_term value = -10 }
				add_faction_goal_slot = { category = long_term   value = -10 }
				TNO_fopo_add_south_american_war_tab = yes
			}
			PAR = {
				add_to_war = {
					targeted_alliance = ARG
					enemy = BRA
				}
			}
			STC = {
				add_to_war = {
					targeted_alliance = ARG
					enemy = BRA
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { TNO_temp_super_event = token:SE_SOUTH_ATLANTIC_WAR }
			TNO_fire_super_event = yes
			set_global_flag = TNO_south_american_war_ongoing

			set_variable = { global.SATW_Escalation = 25 }
			set_variable = { global.SATW_BRA_Exhaustion = 0 }
			set_variable = { global.SATW_ARG_Exhaustion = 0 }

			if = {
				limit = {
					BRA = {
						has_country_leader = {
							character = BRA_Janio_Quadros
							ruling_only = yes
						}

		name = LATAM_news.78.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				is_in_faction_with = GER
				is_in_faction_with = USA
				is_south_american_nation = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Pakt
		name = LATAM_news.78.b
		trigger = {
			is_in_faction_with = GER
		}
	}

	option = { #OFN
		name = LATAM_news.78.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = USA
				is_south_american_nation = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = USA
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = fbi_latam_actions_tt
		}
	}
}
